##  Repository Structure

```sh
└── lab1.3/
    ├── app
    │   └── index.tsx
    ├── app.json
    ├── assets
    │   ├── fonts
    │   └── images
    ├── babel.config.js
    ├── bun.lockb
    ├── components
    │   ├── __tests__
    │   ├── Collapsible.tsx
    │   ├── ExternalLink.tsx
    │   ├── HelloWave.tsx
    │   ├── navigation
    │   ├── ParallaxScrollView.tsx
    │   ├── ThemedText.tsx
    │   └── ThemedView.tsx
    ├── constants
    │   └── Colors.ts
    ├── expo-env.d.ts
    ├── hooks
    │   ├── useColorScheme.ts
    │   ├── useColorScheme.web.ts
    │   └── useThemeColor.ts
    ├── node_modules
    │   ├── .bin
    │   ├── @ampproject
    │   ├── @babel
    │   ├── @bcoe
    │   ├── @egjs
    │   ├── @expo
    │   ├── @graphql-typed-document-node
    │   ├── @hapi
    │   ├── @isaacs
    │   ├── @istanbuljs
    │   ├── @jest
    │   ├── @jridgewell
    │   ├── @nodelib
    │   ├── @npmcli
    │   ├── @pkgjs
    │   ├── @radix-ui
    │   └── @react-native
    ├── package.json
    ├── README.md
    └── tsconfig.json
```

##  Getting Started

###  Prerequisites

**JavaScript**: `version x.y.z`

###  Installation

Build the project from source:

1. Clone the lab1.3 repository:
```sh
❯ git clone lab1.3
```

2. Navigate to the project directory:
```sh
❯ cd lab1.3
```

3. Install the required dependencies:
```sh
❯ npm install
```

###  Usage

To run the project, execute the following command:

```sh
❯ node app.js
```

###  Tests

Execute the test suite using the following command:

```sh
❯ npm test
```

##  Contributing

Contributions are welcome! Here are several ways you can contribute:

- **[Report Issues](https://LOCAL//lab1.3/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `lab1.3` project.
- **[Submit Pull Requests](https://LOCAL//lab1.3/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.
- **[Join the Discussions](https://LOCAL//lab1.3/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your LOCAL account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone lab1.3
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to LOCAL**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
<summary>Contributor Graph</summary>
<br>
<p align="left">
   <a href="https://LOCAL{//lab1.3/}graphs/contributors">
      <img src="https://contrib.rocks/image?repo=/lab1.3">
   </a>
</p>
</details>
